Real-time beamforming process
When *dlSrsSubbandBfAct =true (indicated via HLAPI message* ModulationLinkConf, L1L\_SW\_4859, [11630857: ModulationLinkConf](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_aYtSEvwMEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)), 5G-L1-DL (radio) shall support to calculate real-time (RT) beamforming weight for PDSCH transmission.\*\*

**Note: real-time (RT) beamforming means 5G-L1-DL (Radio) calculate the beam weight vector during PDSCH scheduling based on the SRS channel estimation result provided by 5G-L1-UL (Radio). It is the same concept as DL short-term beamforming at CP2 level.**

The processing for RT beamforming chain is showed in the following diagram:

* W: beamforming weight.
* H: SRS channel estimation.
* NTRX: number of antennas (5G\_L1\_15825\_replaced([11468147](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fBoEFPvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).
* PSRS: number of SRS ports, equals to 4.
* R: rank.
* bfType (beamforming type): beamforming type, indicates by the value of *rtBfUeIndex MSB bits 0~3 of* DlDataFH\_PdschSendReq message (5G\_L1\_IF\_15113\_replaced([11516826](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FSHHAPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).\*\*
* bfMethod (beamforming method): real-time beamforming (RT BF) method, indicated via HLAPI message (*ModulationLinkConf, L1L\_SW\_4859, [11630857: ModulationLinkConf](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_aYtSEvwMEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)).*

**Note: the following figure provides a functional view and is not meant to constrain implementation.**

[Before CB012971-C]

[image-0][image\_desc]The image is a flowchart illustrating the process of PDSCH digital beamforming in a 5G network. The flowchart starts with a "DU" (Distributed Unit) sending a "DIDataFH PdschSendReq message" to "L1 Radio".
The "L1 Radio" block then branches based on "bfType?". If it's "Non-RT BF", it leads to "PDSCH digital beamforming with beam indicates by patternID (L1L\_SW\_2103)". If it's "RT BF", it proceeds to receive a "srsRtBfCeReadyindication message (L1 radio internal message)" and then "Receive srsRtBfCeReadyIndication (CE data) (5G\_L1\_15485)".
From the "Receive srsRtBfCeReadyIndication" block, it goes to "bfSubbandIndex calculation for RT-SB BF (bfType=1) (5G\_L1\_15250)".
There's a decision point "SU-MIMO?" which can be "SU-MIMO" or "MU-MIMO".
If "SU-MIMO", it leads to "bfType& bfMethod?". If "MU-MIMO", it leads to a separate path.
The flowchart then shows different processing paths based on "bfMethod?".
One path is "RT SB BF & MMSE (RZF)", which involves:
- "R SRS ports selection (5G\_L1\_15414)"
- "MMSE (RZF) calculation (5G\_L1\_15312)"
- "BWV normalization (5G\_L1\_15313)"
Another path is "RT SB BF & SVD", which involves:
- "Eigen-vector calculation (5G\_L1\_15102)"
- "Power balance (5G\_L1\_15315)"
- "BWV normalization (5G\_L1\_16655)"
A third path, originating from the "MU-MIMO" branch, involves:
- "SVD-RZF calculation (5G\_L1\_16876)"
- "BWV normalization (5G\_L1\_16877)"
All these paths eventually converge to "EIRP Enabled" or directly feed into the "PDSCH digital beamforming with beam weight Wsl (L1L\_SW\_2103)" block.
There's also a block for "EIRP calculation (5G L1 16395)" which takes "EIRP expansion coefficient" and outputs "DFT beams".
Finally, the "DFT beams" are used in "DFT beams generation at DL carrier setup phase (5G\_L1\_16394)".
The flowchart concludes with a "DIDataFH PdschSendRespPs message" being sent out.
The blocks are labeled with their function and a corresponding ID number in parentheses, e.g., "(5G\_L1\_15485)". The arrows indicate the flow of data and control. The overall diagram depicts a complex signal processing chain for beamforming in a 5G radio interface.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_7966.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

[CB012971-C]

[image-1][image\_desc]The image is a flowchart illustrating the process of PDSCH digital beamforming with beam weight in a 5G network. The flowchart depicts the interactions between different components, including the 5G-L1-DL (BB), 5G-L1-DL (Radio), MU-MIMO Short-term Beam Computer, and SU-MIMO Short-term Beam Computer.
The process starts with a `DIDataFH_UePairingReq` from 5G-L1-DL (BB) to 5G-L1-DL (Radio). The MU-MIMO Short-term Beam Computer receives this request, performs message reception and validation, and then proceeds with SVD-RZF calculation and BWV normalization. Simultaneously, it obtains SRS channel estimation data.
A decision point, "bfType of the UE?", branches the flow based on whether the UE is "Non-RT BF" or "RT SB BF".
For "RT SB BF", the process involves `bfSubbandIndex` calculation for RT-SB BF.
For "Non-RT BF", PDSCH digital beamforming is indicated by `patternID`.
Following this, there's a "SU-MIMO and MU-MIMO selection" step.
The flowchart then details two main paths: SU-MIMO and MU-MIMO.
**SU-MIMO Path:**
This path involves a `bfMethod?` decision, leading to either "MMSE" (RZF) or "SVD".
- **MMSE (RZF):** This involves obtaining SRS channel estimation, R SRS ports selection, MMSE (RZF) calculation, and BWV normalization.
- **SVD:** This involves obtaining SRS channel estimation, Eigen-vector calculation, Power balance, and BWV normalization.
Both MMSE and SVD paths eventually lead to a check for "If EIRP Enabled?". If enabled, an EIRP calculation is performed. If not, or after EIRP calculation, the process continues.
**MU-MIMO Path:**
This path involves obtaining the normalized BF weight per each subband for the UE.
Both SU-MIMO and MU-MIMO paths converge to a step where DFT beams are generated at DL carrier setup phase.
Finally, the process culminates in "PDSCH digital beamforming with beam weight Wsl". The output of this process is `DIDataFH_PdschSendRespPs` (EIRP expansion coefficient).
The flowchart uses various boxes to represent processes and decision points, with arrows indicating the flow of data and control. Some boxes contain specific function names and associated identifiers (e.g., `5G_L1_16876, 11468053`).
The following text elements are present in the image:
- 5G-L1-DL (BB)
- DIDataFH\_UePairingReq
- MU-MIMO Short-term Beam Computer
- 5G-L1-DL (Radio)
- DIDataFH\_UeParingReq message reception and validation in the slot (12631787)
- SVD-RZF calculation (5G\_L1\_16876, 11468053)
- Hkst (PSRS X NTRX) (k=1..K. The K paired UEs)
- Obtain SRS channel estimation (CE) data from dlUeRtBfCebuffer (5G\_L1\_15485,11467878)
- Wal (NTRYX R)
- BWV normalization (5G L1 16877, 11468064)
- DIDataFH\_PdschSendReq
- PDSCH digital beamforming with beam indicates by patternID (L1L\_SW\_2103)
- 0 "Non-RT BF"
- bfType of the UE?
- 1 "RT SB BF"
- bfSubbandIndex calculation for RT-SB BF (5G\_L1\_15250,11467889)
- SU-MIMO
- SU-MIMO and MU-MIMO selection (5G\_L1\_16830,11467908)
- MU-MIMO
- SU-MIMO Short-term Beam Computer
- "MMSE" (RZF)
- bfMethod?
- "SVD"
- Hst (PSRS X NTRX)
- Obtain SRS channel estimation (CE) data from dlUeRtBfCebuffer (5G\_L1\_15485, 11467878)
- Hst (PSRS X NTRX)
- Wsl (NTRXX R)
- R SRS ports selection (5G\_L1\_15414, 11467928)
- Hst (R x NTRX)
- MMSE (RZF) calculation (5G\_L1\_15312, 11467938)
- Wal (NTRXX R)
- BWV normalization (5G\_L1\_15313, 11467955)
- Eigen-vector calculation (5G\_L1\_15102, 11467975)
- Wal (NTRXX R)
- Power balance (5G\_L1\_15315, 11468003)
- Wal (NTRXX R)
- BWV normalization (5G\_L1\_16655, 11468026)
- Wal (NTRXX R)
- Wal (NTRXX R)
- If EIRP Enabled?
- Yes
- Wal (NTRXX R)
- EIRP calculation (5G L1 16395, 11468106)
- DFT beams generated at DL carrier setup phase (5G\_L1\_16394, 11468090)
- DFT beams
- DIDataFH\_PdschSendRespPs (EIRP expansion coefficient)
- PDSCH digital beamforming with beam weight Wsl (L1L\_SW\_2103)
- MU-MIMO
- Obtain the normalized BF weight per each subband for the UE
- Wsl (NTRXX R)[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/img-06161751.png[/image\_path][/image-1]

[End CB012971-C]

Note: due to L1 SMEM allocation limitation, for each CC,   
1. All RTSU UEs shall belong to the same subcell.  
2. In case RTMU UEs occupy only one subcell, RTSU UEs and RT MU UEs shall belong to the same subcell.

**Abbreviation:**

* MMSE: Minimum Mean Squared Error.
* RZF: Regularized Zero-Forcing.

(Note: MMSE is also called as RZF)

* SVD: Singular Value Decomposition
* EIRP: Equivalent Isotropic Radiated Power

5G-L1-DL (Radio) shall also support to calculate the MU-MIMO RT BF weights.

Original diagram can be found here: [CB012971-C DL-real-time beamforming process.vsdx](https://nokia.sharepoint.com/:u:/r/sites/ATFL1Spec/L1%20AS%20documents/Reference%20materials/CB012971/CB012971-C%20DL-real-time%20beamforming%20process.vsdx?d=w648cd325be2b4430a7b1cf8dbb6bd9c3&csf=1&web=1&e=c0ssQu)

11467885: Receiver srsRtBfCeReadyIndication 11467885: Receiver srsRtBfCeReadyIndication 11467885: Receiver srsRtBfCeReadyIndication 11467885: Receiver srsRtBfCeReadyIndication 11467885: Receiver srsRtBfCeReadyIndication 11467885: Receiver srsRtBfCeReadyIndication When dlSubbandBfAct=true (indicated via HLAPI message, L1L_SW_4859) and bfType &gt; 0 (RT-BF, indicates by the value of MSB bits 0~3 of rtBfUeIndex in DlDataFH_PdschSendReq message 5G_L1_IF_15113_replaced( 11516826 )): * 5G-L1-DL (Radio) shall receive the srsRtBfCeReadyIndication for SRS channel estimation (CE) data from 5G-L1-UL (Radio). * 5G-L1-DL (Radio) shall store the SRS channel estimation (CE) data into dlUeRtBfCebuffer structure for real-time beamforming weight calculation. Definiton: * dlBandwidth: NBW, DL cell bandwidth. * bfSubbandSize: beamforming subband size, provided via HLAPI message ( ModulationLinkConf, L1L_SW_4859). The detailed configuration can be found in 5G_CP_ARC_ALG_14229 * numBfSubbands:  equals to ceil(dlBandwidth/bfSubbandSize), indicates the total number of beamforming subbands of the DL bandwidth. * numAntennas =NTRX, see 5G_L1_15825_replaced( 11468147 ). Note: 1. Message srsRtBfCeReadyIndication **is internal between UL and DL, the design and maintainance of this message is per SW preference. Only parts of the message that contain key information are shown here. 2. The description of dlUeRtBfCebuffer structure provides a functional view, the design and maintainance of this structure is per SW preference. Only parts of the structure that contain key information are shown here The example of srsRtBfCeReadyIndication structure is described as below: { Cell_ID (CC_ID). Per UE: - rtBfUeIndex: Unique identifier of the UE. - rnti (debug purpose).- - numSrsPorts: number of SRS ports, in range of [0..3]. - portIndex [numSrsPorts]: sets of SRS port index. - startBfSubbandIndex: the start beamforming subBand index of the current SRS subBand. - numBfSubbands: the number of beamforming subbands of the current SRS subBand. (Note: the parameters startBfSubbandIndex and numBfSubbands are used to define the SRS subBand.) - srsPortPowerportIndex[0]~portIndex[numSrsPorts-1]: the average SRS power over antennas for the current SRS subband for portIndex[0]~portIndex[numSrsPorts-1] with unit dBm. - srsPortPowerOfBfSubbandportIndex[0]~portIndex[numSrsPorts-1][numBfSubbands]: the SRS port power for each beamforming subband, indexed from startBfSubbandIndex to startBfSubbandIndex + numBfSubbands-1. Note: this parameter is reserved and not used. - ceDataBuffportIndex[0]~portIndex[numSrsPorts-1][numBfSubbands][numAntennas]: channel estimation data buffer of portIndex[0]~portIndex[numSrsPorts-1] for - bfSubband [startBfSubbandId..startBfSubbandId+numBfSubbands-1]. } The example of dlUeRtBfCebuffer structure is described as below: Note: key parameters phyCellId, rtBfUeIndex and startBfSubbandIndex are used to obtain the CE data from dlUeRtBfCebuffer structure for the current UE. [image-0][image_desc]The image is a diagram illustrating a hierarchical data structure. The structure is organized into several levels: CC level, UE Level, Port level, and SRS subband level. At the CC level , there are N=[0..3] elements, each represented by a box labeled "CC_0_context" and "CC_N_context", with ellipses indicating intermediate elements. The UE Level has N=[0..15] elements. Each element has a "Key" field, with "Cell ID" shown as an example. This level contains "UE_0" and "UE_N" as examples of specific UE identifiers, with ellipses for others. A dashed arrow from "Cell ID" points to the "UE_0" box, and another dashed arrow points to the "UE_N" box. Below the UE Level, there's another level with a "Key" labeled "rtBfUeIndex". This key is associated with fields like "array" and "rnti". Dashed arrows connect "UE_0" to "rtBfUeIndex" and "UE_N" to "rnti". The Port level shows four ports: "port_0", "port_1", "port_2", and "port_3". Dashed arrows originate from "rtBfUeIndex" and point to "port_0", and from "rnti" to "port_3". The SRS subband level** has N=[0..16] elements, with "srsSubBand_0" and "srsSubBand_N" shown as examples. Dashed arrows connect "port_0" to "srsSubBand_0" and "port_3" to "srsSubBand_N". Further down, within the SRS subband level, there's a key labeled "startBfSubbandInde". This key is associated with fields such as "numBfSubbandssrsPortPower" and "uePortBfCeBuff". A dashed arrow connects "srsSubBand_0" to "startBfSubbandInde". Finally, at the lowest level shown, there's an "addr" field, which is associated with "bfSubbandSrsPortPower[numBfSubbands.ceData[numBfSubbands] [numAnt]". A dashed arrow connects "uePortBfCeBuff" to this "addr" field.[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/img-05121351.png[/image_path][/image-0] Original diagram can be found here: (ID: 11467885)

11467904:
Beamforming subband index calculation
11467904:
Beamforming subband index calculation
Description and rationale: 5G-L1-DL (Radio) shall calculate the beamforming subband index for each allocated PRB(s) for each RT-SB-BF UE.
 
Input:
\* NBW: DL cell bandwidth.
\* bfSubbandSize: beamforming subband size, provided via HLAPI message (ModulationLinkConf, L1L\_SW\_4859).
\* startPrb, numOfPrb, rat0Bitmap, rbgSize, rbgSizeFirst, provided in DlDataFH\_PdschSendReq message.
 
 
 
Definition:
\* PRB\_i: the i\_th allocated PRB, i in range of [0..NBW-1], starts with lowest PRB (PRB 0).
\* bfSubbandIndexPRB\_i: beamforing subband index of PRB\_i(s), starts with value 0.
\* bfType: beamforming type, indicates by rtBfUeIndex MSB bits 0~3 of DlDataFH\_PdschSendReq message (5G\_L1\_IF\_15113\_replaced([11516826](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FSHHAPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).
 
 
Algorithms:
\* IF bfType = 1 (RT-SB BF):
1. 5G-L1-DL (radio) calculate the allocated PRB\_i(s) according to the grant configuration provided in DlDataFH\_PdschSendReq message (5G\_L1\_IF\_15113\_replaced([11516826](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FSHHAPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). For resource allocation type 0, the allocated PRB\_i(s) are calculated according to 5G\_L1\_4258\_replaced([11429959](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e_BcCvvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
2. The BF subband index of each allocated PRB\_i is calculated with the equation below:
bfSubbandIndexPRB\_i= floor (Prb\_i/bfSubbandSize)
 
 
Output:
\* PRB\_i(s): allocated PRB(s)
\* bfSubbandIndexPRB\_i: BF subband index for each scheduled PRB\_i(s).
 
 
Example:
\* The figures are the examples for the mapping between BF subband and allocated PRBs with BF subband size is 2.
 
[Before CB009527-E]
Note: resource allocation RAT1 is not supported for RT-BF PDSCH transmission.
[End CB009527-E]
 
 
[image-0][image\_desc]The image displays three identical tables side-by-side, each representing a resource allocation scheme. Each table has three columns: "PRB index", "bfSubbandIndex", and a third column that varies slightly between the tables but generally indicates UE assignments. The "PRB index" column lists numerical values from 0 to 35, with some rows omitted and indicated by "...". The "bfSubbandIndex" column also contains numerical values, generally corresponding to ranges of PRB indices.
The third column in each table shows assignments to different UEs (User Equipments) and RATs (Radio Access Technologies). These assignments are color-coded: yellow for the "PRB index" column, orange for the "bfSubbandIndex" column, blue for RAT0-UE0, green for RAT0-UE1, and a light blue for RAT1-UE1. Within these colored blocks, letters like 'P', 'D', 'S', 'C', and 'H' are present, likely representing different types of resource allocations or services.
The tables are structured to show how PRB indices are mapped to bfSubbandIndices and then allocated to specific UEs under different RATs. For example, in the first table, PRB indices 34-35 map to bfSubbandIndex 17. PRB indices 32-33 map to bfSubbandIndex 16, which is assigned to UEO: bfSubbandIndex 16 and UE1: bfSubbandIndex 16. PRB indices 30-31 map to bfSubbandIndex 15, assigned to UEO: bfSubbandIndex 15 and UE1: bfSubbandIndex 15. This pattern continues down the table, showing different allocations for different PRB index ranges.
The three tables are visually identical in their structure and content, suggesting they might represent different scenarios or simply a way to present the same information in a comparative manner.

12657118:
SU-MIMO and MU-MIMO algorithm selection
**Description and rationale: 5G-L1-DL (radio) shall select SU-MIMO or MU-MIMO algorithm to calculate  RT-BF weight for each RT-BF UE.**

[Before CB012971-C]

**Input:**

* R&D parameter *rdEnableSbBfDlMuMimoL1 (5G\_L1\_16828\_replaced([11468945](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fBuxx_vvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).*
* rtBfUeIndex: unique identifier of the UE, provided via *DlDataFH\_PdschSendReq message (5G\_L1\_IF\_15113\_replaced([11516826](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FSHHAPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).*
* bfMethod: indicates the real-time beamforming algorithm, provided via HLAPI message (*ModulationLinkConf, L1L\_SW\_4859).*
* bfType: beamforming type, indicates by the value of *rtBfUeIndex MSB bits 0~3 of* DlDataFH\_PdschSendReq message (5G\_L1\_IF\_15113\_replaced([11516826](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FSHHAPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).\*\*
* *rat0Bitmap:* provided in *DlDataFH\_PdschSendReq message (5G\_L1\_IF\_15113\_replaced([11516826](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FSHHAPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).*\*\*
* PRB\_i(s) and bfSubbandIndexPRB\_i: allocated PRBs and the respective BF subband index for each RT-BF UE, see 5G\_L1\_15250\_replaced([11467889](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fBmO7fvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

**Algorithm:**

For RT-BF UEs (bfType = 1) and in the same carrier (identified by physical cell ID):

* **IF rdEnableSbBfDlMuMimoL1 = False:**
* SU-MIMO algorithm is selected.
* **IF rdEnableSbBfDlMuMimoL1 = True** AND *rat0Bitmap =0 (RAT1) for a UE:*\*\*\*\*
* SU-MIMO algorithm is selected.
* **IF rdEnableSbBfDlMuMimoL1 = True, for RT-BF UEs with *rat0Bitmap [image-0][image\_desc]The image is entirely black. There is no discernible content, text, or patterns within the image.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_7973.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]0 (RAT0) and allocated PRB\_i(s) with the related BF subband bfSubbandIndexPRB\_i (5G\_L1\_15250\_replaced([11467889](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fBmO7fvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))):***

-  IF only one RT-BF UE is scheduled in the BF subband:

o SU-MIMO algorithm is selected.

-  IF more than one RT-BF UEs (K UEs) are scheduled in the same PRBs within the BF subband:

o MU-MIMO algorithm is selected.

o 5G-L1-DL (radio) shall build the list for paired UEs (K number UEs, identified by rtBfUeIndex) per each related BF subband. For supported K, see 5G\_L1\_16930\_replaced([11468167](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fBoEGfvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

**Output:**

* RT beamforming algorithm selection.
* In case MU-MIMO RT BF algorithm is selected:

o The list of K paired UEs per related BF subband for MU-MIMO case.

o 5G-L1-DL (radio) shall calculate the MU-MIMO RT-BF weight for the UEs in the paired list using SVD-RZF algorithm as described in 5G\_L1\_16866\_replaced([11468050](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fBndA_vvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

* In case SU-MIMO RT BF algorithm is selected:

o 5G-L1-DL (radio) shall calculate the SU-MIMO beamforming weight for the RT-BF UEs as described in 5G\_L1\_16929\_replaced([11467919](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fBm18_vvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

**Note:**

* All paired UEs share the same FD resource allocation on RBG level, see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_7444\_replaced([11142531](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr4XXvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for details.

[CB012971-C]

**Input:**

* rtBfUeIndex: unique identifier of the UE, provided via *DlDataFH\_PdschSendReq message (5G\_L1\_IF\_15113\_replaced([11516826](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FSHHAPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).*
* bfMethod: indicates the real-time beamforming algorithm, provided via HLAPI message (*ModulationLinkConf, L1L\_SW\_4859).*
* bfType: beamforming type, indicates by the value of *rtBfUeIndex MSB bits 0~3 of* DlDataFH\_PdschSendReq message (5G\_L1\_IF\_15113\_replaced([11516826](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FSHHAPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).\*\*
* *rat0Bitmap:* provided in *DlDataFH\_UePairingReq message ([11517016](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FSIVIfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?vvc.configuration=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/cm/stream/_CqlKNu3yEe-rL47x_rCCmw)).*

**Algorithm:**

For RT-BF UEs (bfType = 1) and in the same carrier (identified by physical cell ID):

* **IF no DlDataFH\_UePairingReq message received OR DlDataFH\_UePairingReq message is dropped due to the exception cases in the slot (see [12631845: DlDataFH\_UePairingReq message validation](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_1jxacDxdEfCYiuaHdt7wgQ?vvc.configuration=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/cm/stream/_CqlKNu3yEe-rL47x_rCCmw)):**
* SU-MIMO algorithm is selected.
* **IF the RT-BF UE is not in any virtualUe in the DlDataFH\_UePairingReq message:**
* SU-MIMO algorithm is selected.
* **IF the RT-BF UE is in virtualUe in the DlDataFH\_UePairingReq message with *rat0Bitmap =0 (RAT1):***
* MU-MIMO algorithm is selected.

**Output:**

* RT beamforming algorithm selection.
* In case MU-MIMO RT BF algorithm is selected:

o 5G-L1-DL (radio) shall calculate the MU-MIMO RT-BF weight for the UEs in the paired list using SVD-RZF algorithm as described in 5G\_L1\_16866\_replaced([11468050](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fBndA_vvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

* In case SU-MIMO RT BF algorithm is selected:

o 5G-L1-DL (radio) shall calculate the SU-MIMO beamforming weight for the RT-BF UEs as described in 5G\_L1\_16929\_replaced([11467919](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fBm18_vvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

**Note:**

* The RT-BF UEs in the same “virtualUe” structure in DlDataFH\_UePairingReq message may have different number of allocated PRBs, see [11142531](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr4XXvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9) for details.

[End CB012971-C]

###### 6.3.6.6.1.2.5 SU-MIMO

###### 6.3.6.6.1.2.5.1 MMSE (RZF) Algorithm

###### 6.3.6.6.1.2.5.1.1 SRS Ports selection

**6.3.6.6.1.2.5.1.1.0-1**  (ID: `11467932`)

SRS Ports selection
Description and rationale: 5G-L1-DL (radio) shall select R SRS ports with highest SRS port power per SRS subBand for each RT-SB-BF UE with "MMSE (RZF)" method:

Input:

* phyCellId.
* R: numOfLayers in DlDataFH\_PdschSendReq message(5G\_L1\_IF\_15113\_replaced([11516826](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FSHHAPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).
* rtBfUeIndex: unique identifier, provided in DlDataFH\_PdschSendReq message (5G\_L1\_IF\_15113\_replaced([11516826](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FSHHAPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).
* dlUeRtBfCebuffer structure: DL CE data buffer, see 5G\_L1\_15485\_replaced([11467878](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fBmO6_vvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
* bfMethod: indicates the real-time beamforming algorithm, provided via HLAPI message (ModulationLinkConf, L1L\_SW\_4859).

Definition:

* bfType: beamforming type, indicates by the value of rtBfUeIndex MSB bits 0~3 of DlDataFH\_PdschSendReq message (5G\_L1\_IF\_15113\_replaced([11516826](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FSHHAPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).
* R\_highestPower\_srsPort0~R-1: the R SRS port index with highest SRS port power.

Algorithms:

* IF bfMethod = 0 ("MMSE (RZF) ") AND bfType = 1 (RT-SB-BF):
* For each SRS subBand:
* 5G-L1-DL (radio) shall select R SRS ports with highest SRS port power,  denoted as R\_highestPower\_srsPort0~R-1, where SRS port index and SRS port power are obtained from dlUeRtBfCebuffer structure (5G\_L1\_15485\_replaced([11467878](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fBmO6_vvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) through the index {phyCellID, rtBfUeIndex, srsPort\_0~srsPort\_3, SRS subBand index).

Output:

* R\_highestPower\_srsPort0~R-1: the R SRS port index with highest SRS port power for each RT-SB-BF UE and each SRS subBand.

---

11467949:
MMSE (RZF) Calculation
Description and rationale: 5G-L1-DL (Radio) shall calculate the MMSE (RZF) beamforming weight per each granted beamforming subband for each RT-BF UE with "MMSE (RZF)" method.

Input:

* bfSubbandIndexPRB\_i: the BF subband index of granted PRB\_i(s), see 5G\_L1\_15250\_replaced([11467889](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fBmO7fvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
* rtBfUeIndex: unique identifier of the UE, provided via DlDataFH\_PdschSendReq message.
* bfMethod: indicates the real-time beamforming algorithm, provided via HLAPI message (ModulationLinkConf, L1L\_SW\_4859).
* NTRX: number of antennas, see 5G\_L1\_15825\_replaced([11468147](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fBoEFPvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
* dlUeRtBfCebuffer structure: DL CE data buffer structure, see 5G\_L1\_15485\_replaced([11467878](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fBmO6_vvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
* R: numOfLayers in DlDataFH\_PdschSendReq message(5G\_L1\_IF\_15113\_replaced([11516826](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FSHHAPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).
* R\_highestPower\_srsPort0~R-1: the R SRS port index with highest SRS port power for each SRS subBand, see 5G\_L1\_15414\_replaced([11467928](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fBm19fvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Definition:

* bfType: beamforming type, indicates by the value of rtBfUeIndex MSB bits 0~3.
* bfSubband\_sl: the sl-th beamforming subband, sl [image-0][image\_desc]The image is entirely black.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_7979.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]bfSubbandIndexPRB\_i (5G\_L1\_15250\_replaced([11467889](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fBmO7fvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

Algorithms:

* IF bfMethod = 0 "MMSE (RZF)" and bfType =1 ("RT-SB-BF"):
* 5G-L1-DL (Radio) shall calculate the beamforming weight with MMSE (RZF) algorithm option2 as described in section §5.1.2.3 of Massive MIMO Algorithm Specification (v3.52, 5G\_L1 16933) for each allocated BF subband bfSubbandIndexPRB\_i.

Where:

1). Hsl: R x NTRX, channel estimation of highest SRS port power for the sl-th BF subband, obtainded from dlUeRtBfCebuffer (5G\_L1\_15485\_replaced([11467878](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fBmO6_vvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) structure through the index {rtBfUeIndex, bfSubband\_sl, R\_highestPower\_srsPort0~R-1}.

2). Wsl: NTRX x R, MMSE (RZF) beamforming weight for the sl-th BF subband.

3). [image-1][image\_desc]The image contains a blurry, abstract design with a gradient of colors, primarily blues, browns, and whites. It appears to be a logo or a graphic element. There is no discernible text or table in the image.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_7979.002.png[/image\_path][/image-1] is defined as the RAD parameter rdMmsePowerFactor (5G\_L1\_15496\_replaced([11468893](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fBuKufvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) with the default value 0.01.

Output:

* Wsl: NTRX x R, beamforming weight for the sl-th BF subband, sl [image-2][image\_desc]The image is entirely black.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_7979.003.png[/image\_path][/image-2]bfSubbandIndexPRB\_i (5G\_L1\_15250\_replaced([11467889](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fBmO7fvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

**Description and rationale: 5G-L1-DL (Radio) shall normalize RT beamforming weight for each allocated BF subband to secure each TRX doesn't exceed maximum transmit power.**

**Input:**

* NTRX: number of antennas, see 5G\_L1\_15825\_replaced([11468147](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fBoEFPvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
* R: *numOfLayers in* DlDataFH\_PdschSendReq message(5G\_L1\_IF\_15113\_replaced([11516826](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FSHHAPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).\*\*
* Wsl: RT beamforming weight of the sl-th beamforming subband with the size NTRX x R (5G\_L1\_15312\_replaced([11467938](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fBm19_vvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). sl [image-0][image\_desc]The image is entirely black.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_7981.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]bfSubbandIndexPRB\_i (5G\_L1\_15250\_replaced([11467889](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fBmO7fvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
* rdParameter rdMmseNorm (5G\_L1\_15511\_replaced([11468901](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fBuKu_vvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

**Algorithms:**

* **IF rdParameter rdMmseNorm =0, Wsl is normalized per layer-wise and per TRX-wise as described in step1 of 5.1.2.3.1 of Massive MIMO Algorithm Specification document  (v3.52, 5G\_L1 16933).**
* per beamforming subband, each beamforming weight vector (columns of Wsl) is first normalized to number of TRX. After that, each TRX (rows of Wsl) is normalized to unity.
* IF rdParameter rdMmseNorm =1, Wsl is normalized per TRX-wise only as described in step2 of  5.1.2.3.1 of Massive MIMO Algorithm Specification.
* per beamforming subband, each TRX (rows of Wsl) is normalized to unity.

**Output:**

* The normalized BF weight [image-1][image\_desc]The image contains the text "Wsl" with a line above the "W". The letters are colorful, with shades of blue, red, and orange. The background is white, and the text is enclosed in a black border.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_7981.002.png[/image\_path][/image-1] (NTRX x R) with the format Q1.0.14 for each allocated beamforming subband.

**Note:**

* 5G-L1-DL (Radio) shall apply the BF weight [image-2][image\_desc]The image contains the text "Wsl" with a line above the "W". The letters are colorful, with shades of blue, red, and orange. The background is white, and the text is enclosed in a black border.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_7981.002.png[/image\_path][/image-2] (NTRX x R) to each BF subband for the current UE, see L1L\_SW\_5401 for details.

**Description and rationale: 5G-L1-DL (Radio) shall calculate the beamforming weight per each granted BF subband with SVD algorithm for each RT-BF UE.**

**Input:**

* bfSubbandIndexPRB\_i: the BF subband index of granted PRB\_i(s), see 5G\_L1\_15250\_replaced([11467889](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fBmO7fvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
* rtBfUeIndex: unique identifier of the UE, provided via *DlDataFH\_PdschSendReq message.*
* bfMethod: indicates the real-time beamforming algorithm, provided via HLAPI message (*ModulationLinkConf, L1L\_SW\_4859).*
* NTRX: number of antennas, see 5G\_L1\_15825\_replaced([11468147](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fBoEFPvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
* dlUeRtBfCebuffer structure: DL CE data buffer structure, see 5G\_L1\_15485\_replaced([11467878](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fBmO6_vvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
* PSRS: number of SRS ports, see 5G\_L1\_15595\_replaced([11467852](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fBmO5_vvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
* R: *numOfLayers in* DlDataFH\_PdschSendReq message(5G\_L1\_IF\_15113\_replaced([11516826](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FSHHAPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).\*\*
* *startPrb,* numOfPrb, *rat0Bitmap,* rbgSize, *rbgSizeFirst, provided in* DlDataFH\_PdschSendReq message.**\***\*

**Definition:**

* bfType: beamforming type, indicates by the value of *rtBfUeIndex MSB bits 0~3.*
* bfSubband\_sl: the sl-th BF subband, sl bfSubbandIndexPRB\_i (5G\_L1\_15250\_replaced(11467889)).

**Algorithms:**

* **IF bfMethod = 1 ("SVD")** AND bfType =1 ("RT-SB-BF"):\*\*\*\*
* 5G-L1-DL (Radio) shall calculate the PSRS eigen vectors*usl,1 ,.., usl,P (P=* PSRS) with SVD algorithm as described in Section §5.1.2.2 and §5.1.2.2.1.1 of Massive MIMO Algorithm Specification (v3.62, 5G\_L1 16933) based on the raw channel estimation Hsl for allocated bfSubband\_sl.\*\*

Where:

1). Hsl: PSRS x NTRX, raw channel estimation for the sl-th BF subband (sl [image-0][image\_desc]The image is entirely black.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_7984.002.png[/image\_path][/image-0]bfSubbandIndexPRB\_i, 5G\_L1\_15250\_replaced([11467889](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fBmO7fvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), obtainded from dlUeRtBfCebuffer (5G\_L1\_15485\_replaced([11467878](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fBmO6_vvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) structure through the index {rtBfUeIndex, bfSubband\_sl}.

2). usl,1 ,.., usl,P: NTRX x 1, the right eigen vectors, calculated according to singular values and the left-singular vectors of Hsl.

3): [image-1][image\_desc]The image is completely black, with no discernible features or content.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_7984.003.png[/image\_path][/image-1]: the respective singular values.

1. 5G-L1-DL (Radio) shall select the R eigen vectors from usl,1,.., usl,P corresponding to the first R (*numOfLayers) largest eigen values ([image-2][image\_desc]The image is entirely black.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_7984.004.png[/image\_path][/image-2]), denoted as BF weight Wsl (NTRX x R) for BF subband bfSubband\_sl.*

**Output:**

* Wsl: size NTRX x R, beamforming weight for for the sl-th BF subband, sl [image-3][image\_desc]The image is entirely black.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_7984.005.png[/image\_path][/image-3]bfSubbandIndexPRB\_i (5G\_L1\_15250\_replaced([11467889](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fBmO7fvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).
* [image-4][image\_desc]The image is completely black, with no discernible features or content.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_7984.006.png[/image\_path][/image-4]: the respective singular values corresponding to Wsl for the sl-th BF subband.

Algorithms: 1. 5G-L1-DL (Radio) shall calculate the power adjustment factor as below: 1). IF  R &lt;= 2 OR rdPowerBalanceMethod = deactivate, power adjustment factor is 1. 2). IF R &gt;2 AND rdPowerBalanceMethod  = "EvShrinkPB", 5G-L1-DL (Radio) shall get the target "coderate 1024" corresponding to the mcs according to the maping table defined in 3GPP 38.214 section 5.1.3.1. * IF the "code rate 1024" is "reserved": * IF mcsTable = 1 "max256QAM": - 5G-L1-DL (Radio) shall calculate the power adjustment factor according to EV shrinking algorithm with the max eigen value ratio target rdMaxEvRatioTargetDb (5G_L1_16663_replaced( 11468938 )) described in section 5.1.2.2.2.3 of 5Gmax Massive MIMO Algorithm specification (v3.62, 5G_L1 16933). * IF mcsTable [image-2][image_desc]The image is entirely black.[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_pukkola_5G_L1_Entity_Level_file_7986.003.png[/image_path][/image-2] 1 "max256QAM": - power adjustment factor is set to 1. * ELSE: * IF the "code rate 1024" &gt; codeRateThreshold: - 5G-L1-DL (Radio) shall calculate the power adjustment factor according to EV shrinking algorithm with the max eigen value ratio target rdMaxEvRatioTargetDb (5G_L1_16663_replaced( 11468938 )) described in section 5.1.2.2.2.3 of 5Gmax Massive MIMO Algorithm specification (v3.62, 5G_L1 16933). * IF "code rate 1024" &lt;= codeRateThreshold: - power adjustment factor is set to 1. Where: * The codeRateThreshold is defined as rdPbCodeRateThresholdRank3 /rdPbCodeRateThresholdRank4 for R (numOfLayers) equals to 3 and 4 respecitvely. * The mapping tables between "code rate*1024" and mcs (5G_L1_IF_15113_replaced( 11516826 )) are defined in 3GPP 38.214 section 5.1.3.1 Table 5.1.3.1-1 /Table 5.1.3.1-2/Table 5.1.3.1-3/Table 5.1.3.1-4 for mcsTable  (provided in DlDataFH_PdschSendReq message, 5G_L1_IF_15113_replaced( 11516826 )) equal to "max64QAM"/"max256QAM"/ "qam64LowSE"/ "max1024QAM" respectively. 2. 5G-L1-DL (Radio) shall apply the power adjustment factor calculated in step 1 to RT beamforming weight Wsl (5G_L1_15102_replaced( 11467975 )). Output: * [image-3][image_desc]The image contains the text "W'si" in a stylized font. The letters are colored with a gradient effect, transitioning from a dark brown to a lighter yellow and then to a light blue. The background is white, and the text is framed by a black border.[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_pukkola_5G_L1_Entity_Level_file_7986.004.png[/image_path][/image-3]l: size NTRX x R, beamforming weight after power balance for each BF subband,  sl [image-4][image_desc]The image is entirely black.[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_pukkola_5G_L1_Entity_Level_file_7986.005.png[/image_path][/image-4]bfSubbandIndexPRB_i (5G_L1_15250_replaced( 11467889 )). * 5G-L1-DL (Radio) shall normalize the RT beamforming weight l per TRX-wise as described in section  5.1.2.2.3 of Massive MIMO Algorithm Specification (v3.62, 5G\_L1 16933).

- per beamforming subband, each TRX (rows of [image-1][image\_desc]The image contains the text "W'si" in a stylized font. 12696571:
Partial allocation on the BF subband
12696571:
Partial allocation on the BF subband
12696571:
Partial allocation on the BF subband
12696571:
Partial allocation on the BF subband
Description: For SU-MIMO and RAT1, 5G-L1-DL (Radio) shall support RT-BF UE allocated on the BF subband with partial PRB(s).

Input:

* bfSubbandSize: beamforming subband size, indicated by [11630855: ModulationLinkConf](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_aYtSEfwMEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9).
* bfMethod: indicates the real-time beamforming algorithm, provided by [11630855: ModulationLinkConf](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_aYtSEfwMEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9).
* subband beamforming weight for each RT-BF UE: computed in [11467938: MMSE (RZF) Calculation](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fBm19_vvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9) or [11467971: SVD Algorithm](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fBm1-_vvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9).
* numOfPrb: indicates in [11516845: PdschGrant](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FSHHBfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9).

Definition:

* bfSubband\_i: the i\_th beamforming subband, starts with value 0.
* dedicated\_bfSubbandUE\_j: the BF subband is allocated to UE\_j only, or UE\_j is allocated on the highest (PRB index) PRB(s) of that subband.
* bfWeightbfSubband\_i,UE\_j: the beamforming weight of bfSubband\_i for UE\_j.
* numOfPrbbfSubband\_i: the number of PRB(s) of the bfSubband\_i, numOfPrbbfSubband\_i is less or equal tobfSubbandSize,

Algorithm:

* In case bfSubband\_M is not the last BF subband, for RT-BF UE1 and RT-BF UE2:
* RT-BF UE\_1 is on the lowest (PRB index) PRB(s) of bfSubband\_M, and the allocated PRB(s) is less than numOfPrbbfSubband\_M, regardless the rest PRB(s) are allocated to other RT-BF UEs or not, 5G-L1-DL (radio) shall find the dedicated\_bfSubband\_iUE\_1, where i is the maximum value less than M, and then apply the BF weight of dedicated\_bfSubband\_iUE\_1 to bfSubband\_M for UE\_1. Note: for RT-BF UEs with RAT 1, because numOfPrb >= bfSubbandSize (see [12686561](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_sbQp0FMyEfCnPp04H8v-AQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9) for details), dedicated\_bfSubband\_iUE\_1 is exist always and up to two RT-BF UEs can allocated on the same BF subband.
* RT-BF UE\_2 is on the highest (PRB index) PRB(s) of bfSubband\_M, and the allocated PRB(s) is less than numOfPrbbfSubband\_M, regardless the rest PRB(s) are allocated to other RT-BF UEs or not, 5G-L1-DL (radio) shall apply the BF weight bfWeightbfSubband\_M,UE\_2to bfSubband\_M for UE2.
* In case bfSubband\_M is the last BF subband, for RT-BF UE1:
* RT-BF UE\_1 is on bfSubband\_M, regardless the allocated PRB(s) equals to or less than numOfPrbbfSubband\_M, 5G-L1-DL (radio) shall apply the BF weight bfWeightbfSubband\_M,UE\_1to bfSubband\_M for UE1.

**Output:**

* Beamforming weight for each RT-BF UE(s).

Example:

* For bfSubband\_1 (case1):
* For UE1, 5G-L1-DL (Radio) shall apply the BF weight of bfSubband\_0UE1 for PRB4~PRB6.
* For UE2, 5G-L1-DL (Radio) shall apply the BF weight of bfSubband\_1UE2 for PRB7.
* For bfSubband\_3 (case2):
* For UE2, 5G-L1-DL (Radio) shall apply the BF weight of bfSubband\_2UE2 for PRB12~PRB14.
* For bfSubband\_0 (case3):
* For UE1, 5G-L1-DL (Radio) shall apply the BF weight of bfSubband\_0UE1 for PRB2~PRB3.
* For bfSubband\_41 (case4, last BF subband):
* For UE3, 5G-L1-DL (Radio) shall apply the BF weight of bfSubband\_41UE3 for PRB160.

[image-0][image\_desc]The image displays two tables side-by-side, each illustrating a mapping between PRB (Physical Resource Block) indices, BF (Beamforming) subband indices, and UE (User Equipment) indices, for different bandwidths: 100MHz on the left and 60MHz on the right.
The left table, for BW: 100MHz, is divided into two main cases: Case 1 and Case 2.
Case 1 covers PRB indices from PRB0 to PRB7.
- PRB0 to PRB3 are mapped to `bfSubband_0` and assigned to UE1.
- PRB4 to PRB7 are mapped to `bfSubband_1` and also assigned to UE1.
Case 2 covers PRB indices from PRB8 to PRB15, and continues with an ellipsis (...) indicating further PRBs up to PRB272.
- PRB8 to PRB11 are mapped to `bfSubband_2` and assigned to UE2.
- PRB12 to PRB15 are mapped to `bfSubband_3` and also assigned to UE2.
The table continues with `bfSubband_4` and ends with `bfSubband_69` for PRB272, with the UE assignments for these further subbands not fully detailed but implied to follow a pattern.
The right table, for BW: 60MHz, is divided into two main cases: Case 3 and Case 4.
Case 3 covers PRB indices from PRB0 to PRB3, and continues with an ellipsis (...) indicating further PRBs.
- PRB0 to PRB3 are mapped to `bfSubband_0` and assigned to UE1.
- Further PRBs are mapped to `bfSubband_2` and assigned to UE2, starting from PRB8 up to PRB11.
Case 4 covers PRB indices from PRB152 to PRB161.
- PRB152 to PRB155 are mapped to `bfSubband_39` and assigned to UE3.
- PRB156 to PRB158 are mapped to `bfSubband_40` and assigned to UE3.
- PRB159 to PRB161 are mapped to `bfSubband_41` and assigned to UE3.
The color coding in the UE Index column highlights the different UE assignments: green for UE1, yellow for UE2, and orange for UE3.

12659681:
SVD-RZF Calculation
12659681:
SVD-RZF Calculation
**Description and rationale: 5G-L1-DL (Radio) shall calculate the beamforming weight with SVD-RZF algorithm for paired (MU-MIMO) RT-BF UEs.**

**Input:**

* rtBfUeIndex: unique identifier of the UE, provided via *DlDataFH\_PdschSendReq message.*
* bfMethod: indicates the real-time beamforming algorithm, provided via HLAPI message (*ModulationLinkConf, L1L\_SW\_4859).*
* NTRX: number of antennas, see 5G\_L1\_15825\_replaced([11468147](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fBoEFPvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
* dlUeRtBfCebuffer structure: DL CE data buffer structure, see 5G\_L1\_15485\_replaced([11467878](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fBmO6_vvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
* PSRS: number of SRS ports, see 5G\_L1\_15595\_replaced([11467852](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fBmO5_vvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
* [Before CB012971-C] R&D parameter rdEnableSbBfDlMuMimoL1[End CB012971-C]
* The list of K paired UEs ([Before CB012971-C] 5G\_L1\_16830\_replaced([11467908](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fBm18fvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) [CB012971-C] in the virtualUe of DlDataFH\_UePairingReq message ([11517016](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FSIVIfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?vvc.configuration=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/cm/stream/_CqlKNu3yEe-rL47x_rCCmw))[End CB012971-C]), per each related BF subband (denoted as bfSubband\_sl, the sl-th BF subband) and for each UEk (identified by rtBfUeIndexk) paired on this subband,
* k=1..K, see 5G\_L1\_16930\_replaced([11468167](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fBoEGfvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)) for supported values.
* Hk,sl: PSRS x NTRX, raw channel estimation for the UE*k  on this sl-th BF subband, obtainded from dlUeRtBfCebuffer (5G\_L1\_15485\_replaced([11467878](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fBmO6_vvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) structure through the index {rtBfUeIndex*k, bfSubband\_sl}.\*\*
* Rk, the *numOfLayers for UEk, provided in* DlDataFH\_PdschSendReq message(5G\_L1\_IF\_15113\_replaced([11516826](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FSHHAPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))\*\*

**Algorithms:**

In case of MU-MIMO mode (see 5G\_L1\_16830\_replaced([11467908](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fBm18fvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), for the paired list, per each related BF subband bfSubband\_sl,

* For each paired UE*k  on bfSubband\_sl:*
* 5G-L1-DL (Radio) shall calculate the Rk right singular vectors*usl,1 ,.., usl,Rk  with FULLEZF algorithm as described in Section §5.1.3.1.3 of Massive MIMO Algorithm Specification (v3.68, 5G\_L1 16933) based on the raw channel estimation Hk,sl.*
* 5G-L1-DL (Radio) shall form the equivalent channel matrix **H**eq,k with the right singular vectors*usl,1 ,.., usl,Rk, the size of* *H**eq,k is Rk x NTRX.****\****\*
* For all the K paired UEs on bfSubband\_sl:
* 5G-L1-DL (Radio) shall form the equivalent channel matrix **H**eq as[image-0][image\_desc]The image is completely black, indicating it is either an empty image or a black screen. There is no discernible content, text, or table present.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_7991.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0](where [ ]T is Transpose operation), the size of **H**eq *is R x NTRX, where* R = *R*1 *+ .. + RK, see 5G\_L1\_16830\_replaced([11467908](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fBm18fvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for supported R.****\******\***
* 5G-L1-DL (Radio) shall calculate MU-MIMO beamforming weight **W**sl (NTRX X R) based on the **H**eq with MMSE algorithm option 2 as described in section 5.1.2.3 of 5GMAX Massive MIMO Algorithm specification (v3.68, 5G\_L1 16933).***\****\*

**Output:**

* The MU-MIMO beamforming weight **W**sl (NTRX X R) for each related BF subband\*\*\*\*

BWV normalization
Description and rationale: 5G-L1-DL (Radio) shall perform linear BWV normalization for the calculated MU-MIMO beamforming weight to avoid transmit power overflow

Input:

* NTRX: number of antennas, see 5G\_L1\_15825\_replaced([11468147](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fBoEFPvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
* R: MU-MIMO layers, R = R1 + .. + RK, where Rk is the numOfLayers (DlDataFH\_PdschSendReq, 5G\_L1\_IF\_15113\_replaced([11516826](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FSHHAPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) of each paired UEs.
* Wsl (NTRX X R): the MU-MIMO beamforming weight for each BF subband, see 5G\_L1\_16876\_replaced([11468053](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fBndBPvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Algorithms:

* 5G-L1-DL (Radio) shall perform the linear normalization to MU-MIMO BF weight Wsl (5G\_L1\_16876\_replaced([11468053](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fBndBPvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) according to section 5.1.3.1.4 of 5GMAX Massive MIMO Algorithm specification (v3.68, 5G\_L1 16933).

Output:

* The normalized BF weight [image-0][image\_desc]The image contains the text "Wsl" with a line above the "W". The letters are colorful, with shades of blue, red, and orange. The background is white, and the text is enclosed in a black border.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_7993.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0] (NTRX x R) with the format Q1.0.14 for each beamforming subband.

Note:

* 5G-L1-DL (Radio) shall obtain the beam forming weight for UEk from [image-1][image\_desc]The image contains the text "Wsl" with a line above the "W". The letters are colorful, with shades of blue, red, and orange. The background is white, and the text is enclosed in a black border.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_7993.001.png[/image\_path][/image-1]  . e.g. the 1st R1 column(s) of [image-2][image\_desc]The image contains the text "Wsl" with a line above the "W". * 5G-L1-DL (Radio) shall apply the BF weight per each BF subband for each paired UEs, see L1L\_SW\_5401 for details.

DFT beam generation
11468102:
DFT beam generation
**Description and rationale: 5G-L1-DL (Radio) shall generate DFT beams at DL carrier setup phase for EIRP (Equivalent Isotropic Radiated Power) expansion coefficient calculation.**

**Input:**

* *dlSubbandBfAct (indicated via HLAPI message, L1L\_SW\_4859, [11630857: ModulationLinkConf](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_aYtSEvwMEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9))*
* **M : *numOfRowTRX , provided via HLAPI message (\*DlArrayState, L1L\_SW\_215, [11630826: DlArrayState](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_aYtSBfwMEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)).***\*
* *N :* numOfColumnTRX, provided via HLAPI message (*DlArrayState, L1L\_SW\_215, [11630826: DlArrayState](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_aYtSBfwMEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)).*\*\*

**Algorithm:**

* 5G-L1-DL (Radio) shall generate DFT beams if *dlSubbandBfAct is active at DL carrier set up phase.*
* Generate the horizontal DFT beams with formula:

[image-0][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation. The equation is:
$WDFTH\_p = [1 \quad e^{j\frac{2\pi p}{N}} \quad e^{j\frac{2\pi p \cdot 2}{N}} \quad ... \quad e^{j\frac{2\pi p \cdot (N-1)}{N}}]$[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_7996.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

N: number of TRX columns; p: horizontal DFT beam index; *p* ∈ *{0, 1, …, N-1}.*\*\*

1. Generate the vertical DFT beams with formula:

[image-1][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation. The equation is:
$WDFTV\_q = [1 \quad e^{j\frac{2\pi q}{M}} \quad e^{j\frac{2\pi q \cdot 2}{M}} \quad ... \quad e^{j\frac{2\pi q \cdot (M-1)}{M}}]$[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_7996.002.png[/image\_path][/image-1],

M: number of TRX rows; q: vertical DFT beam index; *q* ∈ *{0, 1, …, M-1}.*\*\*

1. Construct 2-D DFT beams with formula:

[image-2][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation written in a serif font. The equation is: WDFT\_m = Kron(WDFTV\_q, WDFTH\_p). The text is black and appears on a white background.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_7996.003.png[/image\_path][/image-2],

m: 2D DFT beam index, *m= q*N+p, m *∈* {0, 1, …, N-2, N-1, ..., M*N-1}.*\*\*

**Output**

* 2-D DFT beams.

**Example:**

* For example, for 64 TRX(4x8x2), The TRXs are 4 rows and 8 columns and 2 polarizations. There are 8 DFT beams in horizontal direction and each DFT beam weight vector WDFTHp length is 8.  And there are 4 DFT beams in vertical direction and each DFT beam weight vector WDFTVq is 4. Finally, there are 32 2-D DFT beams for each polarization and the beam weight vector length is also 32.

---

EIRP calculation
11468115:
EIRP calculation
11468115:
EIRP calculation
Description and rationale: 5G-L1-DL (Radio) shall calculate the EIRP (Equivalent Isotropic Radiated Power) expansion coefficient based on the 2D-DFT beams (see 5G\_L1\_16394\_replaced([11468090](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fBndCfvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and the subband beamforming weight (5G\_UP\_ALG\_26924\_replaced([11099691](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_knGlAvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

Input:

* eirpEnable: provided via DlDataFH\_PdschSendReq message (5G\_L1\_IF\_15113\_replaced([11516826](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FSHHAPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).
* R: numOfLayers in DlDataFH\_PdschSendReq message(5G\_L1\_IF\_15113\_replaced([11516826](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FSHHAPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).
* DFT beams weight, see  5G\_L1\_16394\_replaced([11468090](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fBndCfvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
* NTRX: number of antennas (5G\_L1\_15825\_replaced([11468147](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fBoEFPvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).
* [image-0][image\_desc]The image contains the text "Wsl" with a line above the "W". The letters are colorful, with shades of blue, red, and orange. The background is white, and the text is enclosed in a black border.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_7998.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]: NTRX x R, subband beamforming weight BWVs matrix, see 5G\_L1\_15595\_replaced([11467852](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fBmO5_vvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
* bfType: beamforming type, indicates by the value of rtBfUeIndex MSB bits 0~3 in DlDataFH\_PdschSendReq message(5G\_L1\_IF\_15113\_replaced([11516826](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FSHHAPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

Algorithm:

* IF bfType=1 AND eirpEnable=1:
* 5G-L1-DL (Radio) shall select the subband beamforming weight BWVs matrix  [image-1][image\_desc]The image contains the text "Wsl" with a line above the "W". The letters are colorful, with shades of blue, red, and orange. The background is white, and the text is enclosed in a black border.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_7998.001.png[/image\_path][/image-1] (NTRX x R, 5G\_L1\_15595\_replaced([11467852](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fBmO5_vvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) of the 1st BF subband for the scheduled PDSCH.
* 5G-L1-DL (Radio) shall calculate the EIRP expansion coefficient for each BWV per polarization with all DFT beams (5G\_L1\_16394\_replaced([11468090](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fBndCfvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), refer to section 5.1.2.3.3 of 5GMAX Massive MIMO Algorithm specification (v3.67, 5G\_L1 16933) for more details.

Output:

* EIRP expansion coefficient with R\* NTRX elements for each UE with EIRP enable.

##### 6.3.6.6.1.3 RT-BF subband size configuration

**6.3.6.6.1.3.0-3**  (ID: `12696488`)

RT-BF subband size configuration
5G-L1-DL (Radio) shall support the following RT beamforming subband size for PDSCH transmission:

* *bfSubbandSize: indicates the real-time beamforming subband size via HLAPI message ([11630855: ModulationLinkConf](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_aYtSEfwMEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)).*

|  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| L1 Hardware | Technology | PDSCH resource allocation type | bfSubbandSize | First feawture |
| Thor RU | FR1-TDD-eCPRI-7.2e | RAT 0 | {2, 4} | CB009527-A |
| Thor RU | FR1-TDD-eCPRI-7.2e | RAT 1 | {2, 4} | CB009527-E |

**Note:**

**[Before CB009527-I]**

1. In case of SU-MIMO scenario,one beamforming subband can only be occupied by one RT-BF UE.

[CB009527-I]

1. In case of SU-MIMO scenario, 5G-L1-DL (Radio) shall support up to two RT-BF UE(s) allocated on the same BF subband but different PRB(s). See [12696569](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_QOEFsFvBEfCVVMis1D3_Nw?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9) for details.

[End CB009527-I]

2. When total number of BF weights for CSI-RS/PDCCH/WB (wideband beamforming) PDSCH/SB (subband beamforming) PDSCH exceeds the HW limitation of BMUL, 5G-L1-DL (radio) shall drop the rest wideband PDSCH(s).

3: For RAT0, rbgSize in the *DlDataFH\_PdschSendReq message (5G\_L1\_IF\_15113\_replaced([11516826](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FSHHAPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) shall be a multiple of bfSubbandSize.*

##### 6.3.6.6.1.4 RT BF method and type

**6.3.6.6.1.4.0-2**  (ID: `11468141`)

RT BF method and type
5G-L1-DL (Radio) shall support the following RT beamforming configuration for PDSCH transmission:

* bfMethod: indicates the real-time beamforming method via HLAPI message (ModulationLinkConf, L1L\_SW\_4859).
* byType: indicates by the value of rtBfUeIndex MSB bits 0~3 in DlDataFH\_PdschSendReq message(5G\_L1\_IF\_15113\_replaced([11516826](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FSHHAPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

|  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| L1 Hardware | Technology | bfMethod | bfType | First feature |
| Thor RU | FR1-TDD-eCPRI-7.2e | MMSE (RZF) [CB09527-D] , SVD [End CB09527-D] | RT SB BF | CB09527-A |

---

##### 6.3.6.6.1.5 Number of TRX for RT BF calculation

**6.3.6.6.1.5.0-2**  (ID: `11468155`)

Number of TRX for RT BF calculation
The supported number of TRX for RT-BF are as below:

* numTRX: equals to *numOfColumnTRX x* numOfRowTRX x 2 *(polarization),*\*\*
* *numOfColumnTRX and* numOfRowTRX are provided via HLAPI message (*DlArrayState, L1L\_SW\_215).*\*\*

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| L1 Hardware | Technology | number of TRX | First feature |
| Thor RU | FR1-TDD-eCPRI-7.2e | 64 **[CB09527-D]** , 32 **[End CB09527-D]** | CB009527-A |

---

##### 6.3.6.6.1.6 Data precision mode

**6.3.6.6.1.6.0-1**  (ID: `11468163`)

Data precision mode
5G-L1-DL (Radio) shall support the following data precision mode for RT-BF algorithm by setting the rdParameter rdSwitchToLowerPrecision (5G\_L1\_15668\_replaced([11468908](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fBuKvfvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))):

* rdSwitchToLowerPrecision =0:
* Use higher precision data type (vc\_acc\_t) in mxASIP, which has 15 bits mantissa,
* Note: this data type would cost more memory and make the algorithm runs slower.
* rdSwitchToLowerPrecision =1:
* User lower precsion data type(vc\_t) in mxASIP, which has only 7 bits mantissa,
* Note: this data type would cost less memory and make the algorithm runs faster, but the calculation result may have higher EVM

Note: for details of data type in mxASIP, refer to <https://nokia.sharepoint.com/:w:/r/sites/ASIP/_layouts/15/Doc.aspx?sourcedoc=%7Bb4be9329-66c7-455b-ae5f-87c3d76dee4d%7D&action=view&wdAccPdf=0&wdparaid=71871F7D>

---

##### 6.3.6.6.1.7 MU-MIMO Configuration

**6.3.6.6.1.7.0-1**  (ID: `11468172`)

MU-MIMO Configuration
5G-L1-DL (Radio) shall support the following MU-MIMO configuration:

|  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| L1 Hardware | Technology | Max Num of paired UEs per BF subband per slot | Max Num of paired layers per BF subband per slot | First feature |
| Thor RU | FR1-TDD-eCPRI-7.2e | 4 | 8 | CB009527-H |

### 6.3.6.7 PDSCH Power

#### 6.3.6.7.0-1 PDSCH Power Refer to 5G_L1_17364_replaced( 11418175 ) "Tx power scaling EFS (L1 RU chapter)" for PDSCH power adjustment and scaling details. (ID: 12479103)

#### 6.3.6.7.1 PDSCH power balance per beam

##### 6.3.6.7.1.0-1 PDSCH power balance per beam Thor RU (ID: 11468184)

**6.3.6.7.1.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11468188`)

PDSCH power balance per beam
The PDSCH power balance for first beam and second beam are calculated with the following parameters:

* pdschTbTransmitPower: transmit power of the PDSCH transmission in relative dBFS by step of 0.1 dB.
* bestBeamPowerOffset: Best beam power offset by step of 0.1db.

The supported configurations of pdsch power balance per beam are listed in below table. For other configurations not list in the table, bestBeamPowerOffset is set to 0.

|  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Configuration | spatialMode | closedLoop3gppCodebook | numStreamIndex | pdschPrecodingOption4X4 | numOfLayers | bestBeamPowerOffset |
| case A: CL 4x4 with 4-port codebook | “closed loop spatial multiplexing” | "4portTypeICodebook" | 4 | {"PortSelectionUpToRank4 ", "PortSelectionUpToRank4WcsirsPrecoding"} | {3, 4} | [0..150] |
| case B: CL 8x4 with 8-port codebook | “closed loop spatial multiplexing” | "8portTypeICodebook" | 4 | Not used | {3, 4} | [0..150] |

The supported L1 hardwares for PDSCH power balance per beam in Thor is shown in below:

* For TDD FR1:

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| L1 Hardware | case A: power balance per beam for CL 4x4 with 4-port codebook | case B: power balance per beam for CL 8x4 with 8-port codebook |
| Thor RU | [CB009514-F] Supported on TDD-FR1-eCPRI-7.2e [End CB009514-F] | [CB009514-F] Supported on TDD-FR1-eCPRI-7.2e [End CB009514-F] |

For algorithm of PDSCH power balance per beam, refer to 5G\_L1\_10773\_replaced([11416932](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e-TqYPvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

The parameters mentioned above are provided by [CB009514-F] DlDataFH\_PdschSendReq message (5G\_L1\_15113\_replaced([11415123](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e-LuivvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), eCPRI-7.2e) [End CB009514-F].

## 6.3.7 PDSCH capacity

### 6.3.7.0-1 PDSCH capacity UE (grant) Capacity (ID: 11468194)

PDSCH capacity
For Thor RU

---

**6.3.7.0-1.0-1.0-3**  (ID: `11468206`)

PDSCH capacity
Thor RU:

**[CB009843-D, CB009843-WA]**

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| **UE capacity** **(Thor RU)** | **Max DL grants (UEs) per slot per L1 Cell** | **Max DL grants (UEs) per slot per L1 radio** |
| **FR1-TDD-7-2e-eCPRI** | 16 | 64 |

**[End CB009843-D, CB009843-WA]**

**Note:**

**[CB009527-D]**

1. Maximum number of RT-BF (short-term beamforming) UEs per L1 cell is 16, maximum number of RT-BF (short-term beamforming) UEs per slot per L1 cell is 16.
2. 5G-L1-DL (Radio) shall support the capacity of RT-BF UEs above only when the total oBW for cells with IE *dlSrsSubbandBfAct =true in HLAPI message* ModulationLinkConf ([11630857: ModulationLinkConf](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_aYtSEvwMEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)) under this RU is no more than 200 MHz for 64 TRX and 32 TRX.\*\*

**[End CB009527-D]**
